class="_11my0qn"><span class="_1cwnc6v"><span>Contents</span></span><span class="_im0zcz"><svg preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet" height="1em" width="1em" fill="none" 9"/></g></svg></span></div><ul class="_bn6rd2"><li class="_18jxw27"><a class="_8738d6NaN" href="#testimonials"><span class="_1ndgomp">Testimonials</span></a></li><li class="_18jxw27"><a data-editioncontainer="true" class="_ljhfnc"><input type="file" style="display:none"/><div data-slate-editor="true" data-key="3a14615e2c6b4397ba1e4382055d2ee9" contenteditable="false" autoCorrect="on" spellcheck="true" style="outline:none;white-space:pre-wrap;word-wrap:break-word" data-gramm="false"><p class="_v011fo" data-key="d39de4f3d1ac49849499ebbc91dbf24a"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="dbb110b65d514e92b8d8e6661680ba63"><span data-offset-key="dbb110b65d514e92b8d8e6661680ba63-0">Redux is a predictable state container for JavaScript apps.
(Not to be confused with a WordPress framework – </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://reduxframework.com/" target="_blank" data-key="1d58b89d583a4750b0ddbe169e6e44b1"><span data-key="e9c8542af4374ed28c80988e84930208"><span data-offset-key="e9c8542af4374ed28c80988e84930208-0">Redux Framework</span></span></a><span data-key="1bdbfd51d033471eb3aa5927ba1de2f0"><span data-offset-key="1bdbfd51d033471eb3aa5927ba1de2f0-0">.)</span></span></span></p><p class="_v011fo" data-key="961c12d9bcc043cebda1fec880659781"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="5225176c12ff48c1a2f6a4d2075aa4bc"><span data-offset-key="5225176c12ff48c1a2f6a4d2075aa4bc-0">It helps you write applications that behave consistently, run in different environments (client, server, and native), and are easy to test. On top of that, it provides a great developer experience, such as </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://github.com/gaearon/redux-devtools" target="_blank" data-key="0a384a06c0cc44239631ac130809f8c9"><span data-key="6d812fde43bb4e1784cc89d81417aff8"><span data-offset-key="6d812fde43bb4e1784cc89d81417aff8-0">live code editing combined with a time traveling debugger</span></span></a><span data-key="9a00a1e01c224be4a81c4af85c4b3e56"><span data-offset-key="9a00a1e01c224be4a81c4af85c4b3e56-0">.</span></span></span></p><p class="_v011fo" data-key="2a81c32b85aa435697a934c0642a1521"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="b51f12973e574bb0a74992b306f56aa2"><span data-offset-key="b51f12973e574bb0a74992b306f56aa2-0">You can use Redux together with </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://facebook.github.io/react/" target="_blank" data-key="cf519e24eb6042b5bb67b350629b1f16"><span data-key="d30c0cd896ca4da69f298096e9ca8955"><span data-offset-key="d30c0cd896ca4da69f298096e9ca8955-0">React</span></span></a><span data-key="f95307e814c248d9916cebb638e481c0"><span data-offset-key="f95307e814c248d9916cebb638e481c0-0">, or with any other view library.
It is tiny (2kB, including dependencies).</span></span></span></p><div data-slate-void="true"><span style="display:inline-block;vertical-align:top;width:0;color:transparent"><span Really awesome work.”</span></span></a><span data-key="51704f20388349ee8cce8241e1a96ed4"><span data-offset-key="51704f20388349ee8cce8241e1a96ed4-0">
Bill Fisher, author of Flux documentation</span></span></span></p><p class="_k9o3r1h" data-key="022ec527ce9c42e8b270e7aa867a2ccc"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="13992354183042cfade49cb4091a3e9a"><span data-offset-key="13992354183042cfade49cb4091a3e9a-0"><span data-slate-zero-width="true"> </span></span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://twitter.com/andrestaltz/status/616271392930201604" target="_blank" data-key="3f7cf261fc4642308afaaa8258df7cef"><span data-key="80ba246161ac4063898cd71ab2f4d14a"><span data-offset-key="80ba246161ac4063898cd71ab2f4d14a-0">“It&#x27;s cool that you are inventing a better Flux by not doing Flux at all.”</span></span></a><span data-key="72e6d888d5f1408d8176d659042d5ebf"><span data-offset-key="72e6d888d5f1408d8176d659042d5ebf-0">
André Staltz, creator of Cycle</span></span></span></p></blockquote><h1 id="before-proceeding-further" class="_8yc956y" data-key="266e7a15a9864daf8fadbd290eb66f95"><div class="_bc4egv"><span class="_1a3b01i"><span data-key="3ced58f2ad194e06a88be2ed2a441991"><span data-offset-key="3ced58f2ad194e06a88be2ed2a441991-0">Before Proceeding Further</span></span></span><a href="#before-proceeding-further" contenteditable="false" class="_i422ldx"><span class="_15qrizw"><svg preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet" height="1em" width="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" stroke="none" class="_13gjrqj"><g><path d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z" fill-rule="evenodd"/></g></svg></span></a></div><div role="button" tabindex="0" class="_bkzxwn" style="color:#744cbc" contenteditable="false"><svg preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet" height="1em" width="1em" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke="currentColor" class="_13gjrqj"><g><line x1="12" y1="19" x2="12" y2="5"/><polyline points="5 12 12 5 19 12"/></g></svg></div></h1><p class="_v011fo" data-key="5617857fe4ff49b6910c5f5d4b7ae982"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="d86c3cd3027c4da0b43b65d9f9a77adc"><span data-offset-key="d86c3cd3027c4da0b43b65d9f9a77adc-0">Redux is a valuable tool for organizing your state, but you should also consider whether it&#x27;s appropriate for your situation.  Here&#x27;s some suggestions on when it makes sense to use Redux:</span></span></span></p><ul class="_1bj0d8z9" data-key="e1c5321b3f6e420698580a0ddf63001e"><li class=""><div class="_bc4egv" data-key="435085b7fc8e4cf390f72142943e1a5c"><p class="_u2hqaxg" data-key="43e11f7bfe224bb0a4f9f09513bae9da"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="ae4b666db43b42f682b21688fbfe4007"><span data-offset-key="ae4b666db43b42f682b21688fbfe4007-0">You have reasonable amounts of data changing over time</span></span></span></p></div></li><li class=""><div class="_bc4egv" data-key="829c17de6914489190e548fc4ba53207"><p class="_u2hqaxg" data-key="61b6d191d424415f841d02803d9fc98c"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="514a3a02831c44ba9ccc21e46291dff8"><span data-offset-key="514a3a02831c44ba9ccc21e46291dff8-0">You need a single source of truth for your state</span></span></span></p></div></li><li class=""><div class="_bc4egv" data-key="418e5546a0e646549e94b35bc60d7ac0"><p class="_u2hqaxg" data-key="50a6db0e952d400d8bda896be8f1407b"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="e9f8579c8867490d9c1a73b95ec56ef3"><span data-offset-key="e9f8579c8867490d9c1a73b95ec56ef3-0">You find that keeping all your state in a top-level component is no longer sufficient</span></span></span></p></div></li></ul><p class="_v011fo" data-key="556e4d95d30e412c8216adf387788bd1"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="421d217cca384acead7b99e1296923bd"><span data-offset-key="421d217cca384acead7b99e1296923bd-0">Yes, these guidelines are subjective and vague, but this is for good reason. The point at which you should integrate Redux into your application is different for every user and different for every application.</span></span></span></p><blockquote class="_15jhdqa" data-key="ae67b449deba445c89c1c5bd8d6a68fc"><p class="_k9o3r1h" data-key="bd73848a8dae4649b6dac4cd87f0dc17"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="d1fe95ca43a84eb998759d19cbdfac28"><span data-offset-key="d1fe95ca43a84eb998759d19cbdfac28-0"><strong class="_u5j6yl">For more thoughts on how Redux is meant to be used, see:</strong></span><span data-offset-key="d1fe95ca43a84eb998759d19cbdfac28-1">

</span></span></span></p><ul class="_1bj0d8z9" data-key="60826a4e08ad495a8862275a5643e06a"><li class=""><div class="_bc4egv" data-key="8bf32930eea84911b522d144ddd53c22"><p class="_wnv1dqz" data-key="39b901cf32d6436f831934700365b936"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="9f1960f1c9e54f4499b17202a982bb84"><span data-offset-key="9f1960f1c9e54f4499b17202a982bb84-0"><span data-slate-zero-width="true"> </span></span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://medium.com/@dan_abramov/you-might-not-need-redux-be46360cf367" target="_blank" data-key="6a8f439f0d314fcbbfe9e257d62070bc"><span data-key="5694d8031e484c5998fa653d05bf2e0f"><span data-offset-key="5694d8031e484c5998fa653d05bf2e0f-0"><strong class="_u5j6yl">You Might Not Need Redux</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="9da9c6d59ae34f14bedc1e981e667375"><span data-offset-key="9da9c6d59ae34f14bedc1e981e667375-0">

</span></span></span></p></div></li><li class=""><div class="_bc4egv" data-key="bb939c258a2940bd81cf3b4e425ae1e0"><p class="_wnv1dqz" data-key="f4877a2da87042ee9bc10c9cc25d6a02"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="a48c35a17c184416a2c735a822e63d3d"><span data-offset-key="a48c35a17c184416a2c735a822e63d3d-0"><span data-slate-zero-width="true"> </span></span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="http://blog.isquaredsoftware.com/2017/05/idiomatic-redux-tao-of-redux-part-1/" target="_blank" data-key="9145b7f41de445ae8c4d1af2605065ef"><span data-key="7827249b2be74f06b449679ddb7b4e76"><span data-offset-key="7827249b2be74f06b449679ddb7b4e76-0"><strong class="_u5j6yl">The Tao of Redux, Part 1 - Implementation and Intent</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="3a512c662aa54c8996270c52f1424556"><span data-offset-key="3a512c662aa54c8996270c52f1424556-0">

</span></span></span></p></div></li><li class=""><div class="_bc4egv" data-key="064092b1675642fe94a6c03dabc6fcc7"><p class="_wnv1dqz" data-key="b2c3b481d9d040d6a2668f3c91ded384"><span class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="http://blog.isquaredsoftware.com/2017/05/idiomatic-redux-tao-of-redux-part-2/" target="_blank" data-key="b2ab85ffcd304a5fac06d33f96a3ad2a"><span Philosophy</strong></span></span></a><span data-key="dad170ecc78945ebb1385a4ba9bd2740"><span data-offset-key="dad170ecc78945ebb1385a4ba9bd2740-0"><span data-slate-zero-width="true"> </span></span></span></span></p></div></li><li class=""><div class="_bc4egv" data-key="d6bae5fb15e14ac8abb55ec60f1bde4e"><p class="_wnv1dqz" data-slate-zero-width="true"> </span></span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://redux.js.org/faq" target="_blank" data-key="d3246ba0706e4b4fb279a29dcfcc0a9d"><span data-slate-zero-width="true"> </span></span></span></span></p></div></li></ul></blockquote><h1 id="developer-experience" class="_8yc956y" data-key="53baf4ed4e82478abdeed673e9bbaba0"><div class="_bc4egv"><span class="_1a3b01i"><span data-key="4e92fdfdde794c7db74ad94b7187ccd1"><span data-offset-key="4e92fdfdde794c7db74ad94b7187ccd1-0">Developer Experience</span></span></span><a href="#developer-experience" contenteditable="false" class="_i422ldx"><span class="_15qrizw"><svg preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet" height="1em" width="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 16 16" meet" height="1em" width="1em" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke="currentColor" class="_13gjrqj"><g><line x1="12" y1="19" x2="12" y2="5"/><polyline points="5 12 12 5 19 12"/></g></svg></div></h1><p class="_v011fo" data-key="50b80bc51bf049fab401706932df18f9"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="6d9331937f7d41e4b0b88125a4e94029"><span data-offset-key="6d9331937f7d41e4b0b88125a4e94029-0">Dan Abramov (author of Redux) wrote Redux while working on his React Europe talk called </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=xsSnOQynTHs" target="_blank" data-key="e70a6f2a90594ef99ea7aa622a335d03"><span data-key="4213edb807304c8c976371bdb7c9ea3e"><span data-offset-key="4213edb807304c8c976371bdb7c9ea3e-0">“Hot Reloading with Time Travel”</span></span></a><span data-key="a3639154519d474bba699b2227f5f6a4"><span data-offset-key="a3639154519d474bba699b2227f5f6a4-0">. His goal was to create a state management library with minimal API but completely predictable behavior, so it is possible to implement logging, hot reloading, time travel, universal apps, record and replay, without any buy-in from the developer.</span></span></span></p><h1 id="influences" class="_8yc956y" data-key="e86a00f76cb043b2932b6d40117ee2cb"><div class="_bc4egv"><span class="_1a3b01i"><span data-key="03dbe441a08b43debec165b84e8f68dd"><span data-offset-key="03dbe441a08b43debec165b84e8f68dd-0">Influences</span></span></span><a href="#influences" contenteditable="false" class="_i422ldx"><span class="_15qrizw"><svg preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet" height="1em" width="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" stroke="none" class="_13gjrqj"><g><path d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z" fill-rule="evenodd"/></g></svg></span></a></div><div role="button" tabindex="0" class="_bkzxwn" style="color:#744cbc" contenteditable="false"><svg preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet" height="1em" width="1em" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke="currentColor" class="_13gjrqj"><g><line x1="12" y1="19" x2="12" y2="5"/><polyline points="5 12 12 5 19 12"/></g></svg></div></h1><p class="_v011fo" data-key="d4e2a4ce881e499d8592da388db11ef6"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="55eac4ed900343328389bdcf7f2243c3"><span data-offset-key="55eac4ed900343328389bdcf7f2243c3-0">Redux evolves the ideas of </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="http://facebook.github.io/flux/" target="_blank" data-key="fddcec5053e34273ad652a564b2a533a"><span data-key="915714f2606245ef8aa0961222e3a13f"><span data-offset-key="915714f2606245ef8aa0961222e3a13f-0">Flux</span></span></a><span data-key="8637b30b5cb24af48244294fe36f85de"><span data-offset-key="8637b30b5cb24af48244294fe36f85de-0">, but avoids its complexity by taking cues from </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://github.com/evancz/elm-architecture-tutorial/" target="_blank" data-key="87697cce8e404125bced734759781d6a"><span data-key="47c77dc22f0b4b8fa2dfea4141f05551"><span data-offset-key="47c77dc22f0b4b8fa2dfea4141f05551-0">Elm</span></span></a><span data-key="5c84125d14ff4e92b0b32fb6a00bc61e"><span data-offset-key="5c84125d14ff4e92b0b32fb6a00bc61e-0">.
Whether you have used them or not, Redux only takes a few minutes to get started with.</span></span></span></p><h1 id="installation" class="_8yc956y" data-key="9bd9e43611da4de2906eff4ba3d5bf35"><div class="_bc4egv"><span class="_1a3b01i"><span data-key="263b7b9cf52d4fb48127632fc6cc25e3"><span data-offset-key="263b7b9cf52d4fb48127632fc6cc25e3-0">Installation</span></span></span><a href="#installation" contenteditable="false" class="_i422ldx"><span class="_15qrizw"><svg preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet" height="1em" width="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" stroke="none" class="_13gjrqj"><g><path d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z" fill-rule="evenodd"/></g></svg></span></a></div><div role="button" tabindex="0" class="_bkzxwn" style="color:#744cbc" contenteditable="false"><svg preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet" height="1em" width="1em" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke="currentColor" class="_13gjrqj"><g><line x1="12" y1="19" x2="12" y2="5"/><polyline points="5 12 12 5 19 12"/></g></svg></div></h1><p class="_v011fo" data-key="523766e440ab4c34a90bc95ca91dc692"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="daf3f9a37ba34f63a4ca900f723660f2"><span data-offset-key="daf3f9a37ba34f63a4ca900f723660f2-0">To install the stable version:</span></span></span></p><div class="_1m3v4sx"><div class="_1qznkvsr" contenteditable="false"><div role="button" tabindex="-1" class="_1uona6bNaN" aria-label="Copy"><svg preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet" height="1em" width="1em" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke="currentColor" class="_13gjrqj"><g><rect x="9" y="9" width="13" height="13" rx="2" ry="2"/><path d="M5 15H4a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V4a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h9a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v1"/></g></svg></div></div><div data-key="f59baf51bd9c4cc2a0c9cece030f8e07"><div><pre class="_18pa1io" spellcheck="false" data-key="65e1c36250a04469831727085b61cdcd"><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="c5f20bf945444fb7ab2222f2f6c4ec62"><span data-key="ef9aa17941964b68bbc69d25ae1a3d70"><span data-offset-key="ef9aa17941964b68bbc69d25ae1a3d70-0">npm install --save redux</span></span></div></pre></div></div></div><p class="_v011fo" data-key="c0660f4d37614bcdb5570681e56b6fd1"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="078bd4a9fd904b348faae4feefc4bcfa"><span data-offset-key="078bd4a9fd904b348faae4feefc4bcfa-0">This assumes you are using </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://www.npmjs.com/" target="_blank" data-key="85815a49dcda46e48a551c1700ea61c2"><span data-key="ac1c5adf236844d0bbc1389d3aa6b749"><span data-offset-key="ac1c5adf236844d0bbc1389d3aa6b749-0">npm</span></span></a><span data-key="afa1e51ab40e43348b3fba689a213413"><span data-offset-key="afa1e51ab40e43348b3fba689a213413-0"> as your package manager.</span></span></span></p><p class="_v011fo" data-key="f21710ad78ae4740a42b9a5a9180840a"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="506613260a3742398bcda23e8df4287d"><span data-offset-key="506613260a3742398bcda23e8df4287d-0">If you&#x27;re not, you can </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://unpkg.com/redux/" target="_blank" data-key="fb74f0f262984c208d501d713f8508c4"><span data-key="f7f37ca1544843cf8ce753b67d15beec"><span data-offset-key="f7f37ca1544843cf8ce753b67d15beec-0">access these files on unpkg</span></span></a><span data-key="1498abb9ea8547ed90780a1c41751478"><span data-offset-key="1498abb9ea8547ed90780a1c41751478-0">, download them, or point your package manager to them.</span></span></span></p><p class="_v011fo" data-key="0f09ffa7b78e4014bd8cf43bd1af7685"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="382d426d9d2b4eedac740acda9270729"><span data-offset-key="382d426d9d2b4eedac740acda9270729-0">Most commonly people consume Redux as a collection of </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="http://webpack.github.io/docs/commonjs.html" target="_blank" data-key="f7ec362bb4fc4b07ad73ce08883ced88"><span data-key="ad7dd5d9d6664aac87f2d15f7e4f6b91"><span data-offset-key="ad7dd5d9d6664aac87f2d15f7e4f6b91-0">CommonJS</span></span></a><span data-key="0b742f61b7b645379c1a29718003278d"><span data-offset-key="0b742f61b7b645379c1a29718003278d-0"> modules. These modules are what you get when you import </span><span data-offset-key="0b742f61b7b645379c1a29718003278d-1"><code spellcheck="false" class="_dy325n">redux</code></span><span data-offset-key="0b742f61b7b645379c1a29718003278d-2"> in a </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://webpack.js.org/" target="_blank" data-key="ae11b2a4bae142c0894074a5d332a725"><span data-key="3793e0171bd14f0cafe39ec95a624b77"><span data-offset-key="3793e0171bd14f0cafe39ec95a624b77-0">Webpack</span></span></a><span data-key="01fa94eefa5d49748510801a2d063823"><span data-offset-key="01fa94eefa5d49748510801a2d063823-0">, </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="http://browserify.org/" target="_blank" data-key="be242d7471dd49148589622785fa8713"><span data-key="7db7891c6dcc420caf9a21d53eb05dab"><span data-offset-key="7db7891c6dcc420caf9a21d53eb05dab-0">Browserify</span></span></a><span data-key="4bb47456e4f84179a214333fd19ac578"><span data-offset-key="4bb47456e4f84179a214333fd19ac578-0">, or a Node environment. If you like to live on the edge and use </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="http://rollupjs.org" target="_blank" data-key="4e389290cc2b423fa60dad2ef5233273"><span data-key="bff251d6fa754b1d820008c6e0d153dd"><span data-offset-key="bff251d6fa754b1d820008c6e0d153dd-0">Rollup</span></span></a><span data-key="5ff8c2f902404bfbbf086cd76731fb8f"><span data-offset-key="5ff8c2f902404bfbbf086cd76731fb8f-0">, we support that as well.</span></span></span></p><p class="_v011fo" data-key="39770d95b1d04b77b4b82a48ffbba23f"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="c9c002fc646447c395716919a340ed07"><span data-offset-key="c9c002fc646447c395716919a340ed07-0">If you don&#x27;t use a module bundler, it&#x27;s also fine. The </span><span data-offset-key="c9c002fc646447c395716919a340ed07-1"><code spellcheck="false" class="_dy325n">redux</code></span><span data-offset-key="c9c002fc646447c395716919a340ed07-2"> npm package includes precompiled production and development </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://github.com/umdjs/umd" target="_blank" data-key="9dc5ac62dc6f40a89ef0612de6ec2ab8"><span data-key="0dd9a1981cf44ec29631cd360c0728e9"><span data-offset-key="0dd9a1981cf44ec29631cd360c0728e9-0">UMD</span></span></a><span data-key="88b9bab9428c463585a3b5746d0e9964"><span data-offset-key="88b9bab9428c463585a3b5746d0e9964-0"> builds in the </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://unpkg.com/redux/dist/" target="_blank" data-key="0b95efe59a584589ba62f6620a13967d"><span data-key="f42c5b9c19354ed899d438be79520a5d"><span data-offset-key="f42c5b9c19354ed899d438be79520a5d-0"><code spellcheck="false" class="_dy325n">dist</code></span><span data-offset-key="f42c5b9c19354ed899d438be79520a5d-1"> folder</span></span></a><span data-key="9ce7759e622f4233846ed337563c4993"><span data-offset-key="9ce7759e622f4233846ed337563c4993-0">. They can be used directly without a bundler and are thus compatible with many popular JavaScript module loaders and environments. For example, you can drop a UMD build as a </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://unpkg.com/redux/dist/redux.js" target="_blank" data-key="9556990175c547c38253353aa913511a"><span data-key="d3c9b0a1a9004958a9336d1fd087fc3e"><span data-offset-key="d3c9b0a1a9004958a9336d1fd087fc3e-0"><code spellcheck="false" class="_dy325n">&lt;script&gt;</code></span><span data-offset-key="d3c9b0a1a9004958a9336d1fd087fc3e-1"> tag</span></span></a><span data-key="6fc6089ab4114cf3a664d0efaad59450"><span data-offset-key="6fc6089ab4114cf3a664d0efaad59450-0"> on the page, or </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://github.com/reactjs/redux/pull/1181#issuecomment-167361975" target="_blank" data-key="b4bc3782495f49978ed8f1a31bcc281e"><span data-key="e2bdba35eeaa43b8b57a3ebb5aea1226"><span data-offset-key="e2bdba35eeaa43b8b57a3ebb5aea1226-0">tell Bower to install it</span></span></a><span data-key="b3419ff2213849e99d46b0eb554926b2"><span data-offset-key="b3419ff2213849e99d46b0eb554926b2-0">. The UMD builds make Redux available as a </span><span data-offset-key="b3419ff2213849e99d46b0eb554926b2-1"><code spellcheck="false" class="_dy325n">window.Redux</code></span><span data-offset-key="b3419ff2213849e99d46b0eb554926b2-2"> global variable.</span></span></span></p><p class="_v011fo" data-key="cd4f89ae2a8642b09d8a3615cf095567"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="be8bf1a7df0e435ab0d0eed0190f12ad"><span data-offset-key="be8bf1a7df0e435ab0d0eed0190f12ad-0">The Redux source code is written in ES2015 but we precompile both CommonJS and UMD builds to ES5 so they work in </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="http://caniuse.com/#feat=es5" target="_blank" data-key="6c85aab3b5274d5ea81388d48a63ca78"><span data-key="265ed4b4aa464a90a22ec282976524f6"><span data-offset-key="265ed4b4aa464a90a22ec282976524f6-0">any modern browser</span></span></a><span data-key="cb63ffe393c94761b67d1cecebbf8229"><span data-offset-key="cb63ffe393c94761b67d1cecebbf8229-0">. You don&#x27;t need to use Babel or a module bundler to </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://github.com/reactjs/redux/blob/master/examples/counter-vanilla/index.html" target="_blank" data-key="348dff3187f04477b49eda11a9b59028"><span data-key="7870a160501444afb267ea56adec7777"><span data-offset-key="7870a160501444afb267ea56adec7777-0">get started with Redux</span></span></a><span data-key="94d02f80e3a843c6acb8384a7019434e"><span data-offset-key="94d02f80e3a843c6acb8384a7019434e-0">.</span></span></span></p><h2 id="complementary-packages" class="_1r75zq6v" data-key="05d5b6c8c5ef447a9e73ab3d614fcea2"><div class="_bc4egv"><span class="_10vjbea"><span data-key="32326444229144aa8a6abd0192bd9273"><span data-offset-key="32326444229144aa8a6abd0192bd9273-0">Complementary Packages</span></span></span><a href="#complementary-packages" contenteditable="false" class="_i422ldx"><span class="_15qrizw"><svg preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet" height="1em" width="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" stroke="none" class="_13gjrqj"><g><path d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z" fill-rule="evenodd"/></g></svg></span></a></div></h2><p class="_v011fo" data-key="52aef0ca5ac741aeac6a442c54a70536"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="a39cfd8822104322ab2e57cdc6c6b88e"><span data-offset-key="a39cfd8822104322ab2e57cdc6c6b88e-0">Most likely, you&#x27;ll also need </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://github.com/reactjs/react-redux" target="_blank" data-key="711c188eac5f4f3caf4b0c8dd26163b9"><span data-key="9ff7f8f619664327a7e22dbaa99bdff0"><span data-offset-key="9ff7f8f619664327a7e22dbaa99bdff0-0">the React bindings</span></span></a><span data-key="e08af64a928a4be1a86aa768335937a7"><span data-offset-key="e08af64a928a4be1a86aa768335937a7-0"> and </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://github.com/gaearon/redux-devtools" target="_blank" data-key="ff1652d6c7df4640bec7fd98bbaed4a3"><span data-key="c4ec230b24fe43e9ac3de03a75b0ae8f"><span data-offset-key="c4ec230b24fe43e9ac3de03a75b0ae8f-0">the developer tools</span></span></a><span data-key="9977fd60e15d49918a0b4b688b675f13"><span data-offset-key="9977fd60e15d49918a0b4b688b675f13-0">.</span></span></span></p><div class="_1m3v4sx"><div class="_1qznkvsr" contenteditable="false"><div role="button" tabindex="-1" class="_1uona6bNaN" aria-label="Copy"><svg preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet" height="1em" width="1em" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke="currentColor" class="_13gjrqj"><g><rect x="9" y="9" width="13" height="13" rx="2" ry="2"/><path d="M5 15H4a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V4a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h9a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v1"/></g></svg></div></div><div data-key="d5e73227967c469ca8b9d032b3b31fbb"><div><pre class="_18pa1io" spellcheck="false" data-key="30b41d7728d94fa7b9d1ca5121b3655b"><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="94e8ace5c5ab46849aa3ad6b05e38e7d"><span data-key="dd120ae4bb6f410fbfec5c772eb2a973"><span data-offset-key="dd120ae4bb6f410fbfec5c772eb2a973-0">npm install --save react-redux</span></span></div><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="ebcf9bf1ae26476e886f879a14ed258d"><span data-key="78a4a69c4fea493180c92c7e495e19e1"><span data-offset-key="78a4a69c4fea493180c92c7e495e19e1-0">npm install --save-dev redux-devtools</span></span></div></pre></div></div></div><p class="_v011fo" data-key="be8aa58feb0f4df48b41ec2bca97a29a"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="c917843d297e450e8eeb3d585463386d"><span data-offset-key="c917843d297e450e8eeb3d585463386d-0">Note that unlike Redux itself, many packages in the Redux ecosystem don&#x27;t provide UMD builds, so we recommend using CommonJS module bundlers like </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="https://webpack.js.org/" target="_blank" data-key="e8e2bb9a58ab4bde8e98944d7969ae84"><span data-key="1925031463424a7895f28714d9c6c558"><span data-offset-key="1925031463424a7895f28714d9c6c558-0">Webpack</span></span></a><span data-key="ada4ee6281f14b6c9f338b247eea822d"><span data-offset-key="ada4ee6281f14b6c9f338b247eea822d-0"> and </span></span><a class="_1pk4jlv" style="color:#744cbc" href="http://browserify.org/" target="_blank" data-key="19a1da825ff749fc8735558869d040e8"><span data-key="579300cf967b4ad99e9e6ac0d792e222"><span data-offset-key="579300cf967b4ad99e9e6ac0d792e222-0">Browserify</span></span></a><span data-key="b282dc5ccc4c4e4d8652a18a1529befd"><span data-offset-key="b282dc5ccc4c4e4d8652a18a1529befd-0"> for the most comfortable development experience.</span></span></span></p><h1 id="the-gist" class="_8yc956y" data-key="3d78e46a485f4f3db492eb417205297b"><div class="_bc4egv"><span class="_1a3b01i"><span data-key="8ced56b83e5c40d89a345ef744c57e58"><span data-offset-key="8ced56b83e5c40d89a345ef744c57e58-0">The Gist</span></span></span><a href="#the-gist" contenteditable="false" class="_i422ldx"><span class="_15qrizw"><svg preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet" height="1em" width="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" stroke="none" class="_13gjrqj"><g><path d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z" fill-rule="evenodd"/></g></svg></span></a></div><div role="button" tabindex="0" class="_bkzxwn" style="color:#744cbc" contenteditable="false"><svg preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet" height="1em" width="1em" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke="currentColor" class="_13gjrqj"><g><line x1="12" y1="19" x2="12" y2="5"/><polyline points="5 12 12 5 19 12"/></g></svg></div></h1><p class="_v011fo" data-key="c00737afb3074b26a1a5e72e37729109"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="a8b91359bfa948cea512a76759f050f3"><span data-offset-key="a8b91359bfa948cea512a76759f050f3-0">The whole state of your app is stored in an object tree inside a single </span><span data-offset-key="a8b91359bfa948cea512a76759f050f3-1"><em>store</em></span><span data-offset-key="a8b91359bfa948cea512a76759f050f3-2">.
The only way to change the state tree is to emit an </span><span data-offset-key="a8b91359bfa948cea512a76759f050f3-3"><em>action</em></span><span data-offset-key="a8b91359bfa948cea512a76759f050f3-4">, an object describing what happened.
To specify how the actions transform the state tree, you write pure </span><span data-offset-key="a8b91359bfa948cea512a76759f050f3-5"><em>reducers</em></span><span data-offset-key="a8b91359bfa948cea512a76759f050f3-6">.</span></span></span></p><p class="_v011fo" data-key="10733864f80740b08f60bbd982f51f11"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="4d97357386844b68b5896b01153c9050"><span data-offset-key="4d97357386844b68b5896b01153c9050-0">That&#x27;s it!</span></span></span></p><div class="_1m3v4sx"><div class="_1qznkvsr" contenteditable="false"><div role="button" tabindex="-1" class="_1uona6bNaN" aria-label="Copy"><svg preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet" height="1em" width="1em" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke="currentColor" class="_13gjrqj"><g><rect x="9" y="9" width="13" height="13" rx="2" ry="2"/><path d="M5 15H4a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V4a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h9a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v1"/></g></svg></div></div><div data-key="e6e6c3bc7a24468a93ed8b24cc32bf91"><div><pre class="_18pa1io" spellcheck="false" data-key="8d126cbdef3347ff8061715e2b342a6d"><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="53aef74c9dc7428ca5e82ec0c08b22ed"><span data-key="6a197d305b254c3b854463c174e65c56"><span data-offset-key="6a197d305b254c3b854463c174e65c56-0"><span class="prism-token token  keyword ">import</span></span><span data-offset-key="6a197d305b254c3b854463c174e65c56-1"> </span><span data-offset-key="6a197d305b254c3b854463c174e65c56-2"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">{</span></span><span data-offset-key="6a197d305b254c3b854463c174e65c56-3"> createStore </span><span data-offset-key="6a197d305b254c3b854463c174e65c56-4"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">}</span></span><span data-offset-key="6a197d305b254c3b854463c174e65c56-5"> </span><span data-offset-key="6a197d305b254c3b854463c174e65c56-6"><span class="prism-token token  keyword ">from</span></span><span data-offset-key="6a197d305b254c3b854463c174e65c56-7"> </span><span data-offset-key="6a197d305b254c3b854463c174e65c56-8"><span class="prism-token token  string ">&#x27;redux&#x27;</span></span></span></div><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="07f37d911ff5417f9907b57a254dce6a"><span data-key="21bfbd46dfbe426198f0833d0fc9ba8f"><span data-offset-key="21bfbd46dfbe426198f0833d0fc9ba8f-0"><span data-slate-zero-width="true"> </span></span></span></div><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="24e3f5fd17054e899d98a4c62898a2c9"><span data-key="5b6a06a5021f4d3e9bb8d5f1a9b6d3f7"><span data-offset-key="5b6a06a5021f4d3e9bb8d5f1a9b6d3f7-0"><span class="prism-token token  comment ">/**</span></span></span></div><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="513b2e844f5d47a0b099e0e6b9ac92b0"><span data-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15"><span data-offset-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15-0"> </span><span data-offset-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15-1"><span class="prism-token token  operator ">*</span></span><span data-offset-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15-2"> This is a reducer</span><span data-offset-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15-3"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">,</span></span><span data-offset-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15-4"> a pure </span><span data-offset-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15-5"><span class="prism-token token  keyword ">function</span></span><span data-offset-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15-6"> </span><span data-offset-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15-7"><span class="prism-token token  keyword ">with</span></span><span data-offset-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15-8"> </span><span data-offset-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15-9"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">(</span></span><span data-offset-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15-10">state</span><span data-offset-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15-11"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">,</span></span><span data-offset-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15-12"> action</span><span data-offset-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15-13"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">)</span></span><span data-offset-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15-14"> </span><span data-offset-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15-15"><span class="prism-token token  operator ">=&gt;</span></span><span data-offset-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15-16"> state signature</span><span data-offset-key="e34d4e8dbbcb4654bd65ec125d6aea15-17"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">.</span></span></span></div><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="fe112dad1fa8426b980d835736238802"><span data-key="d28f017368f5490db19e960c4be58bb9"><span data-offset-key="d28f017368f5490db19e960c4be58bb9-0"> </span><span data-offset-key="d28f017368f5490db19e960c4be58bb9-1"><span class="prism-token token  operator ">*</span></span><span data-offset-key="d28f017368f5490db19e960c4be58bb9-2"> It describes how an action transforms the state into the next state</span><span data-offset-key="d28f017368f5490db19e960c4be58bb9-3"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">.</span></span></span></div><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="eaf8bc2a8d834f25af5756e32926fa0e"><span data-key="e8cbfd2829ed4a1ba7728cac89b7f1c1"><span data-offset-key="e8cbfd2829ed4a1ba7728cac89b7f1c1-0"> </span><span data-offset-key="e8cbfd2829ed4a1ba7728cac89b7f1c1-1"><span class="prism-token token  operator ">*</span></span></span></div><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="414a29e1e8ab45df8ea4c670b8bf8711"><span data-key="28b25ed728244913959d1dee06472aec"><span data-offset-key="28b25ed728244913959d1dee06472aec-0"> </span><span data-offset-key="28b25ed728244913959d1dee06472aec-1"><span class="prism-token token  operator ">*</span></span><span data-offset-key="28b25ed728244913959d1dee06472aec-2"> The shape </span><span data-offset-key="64d6b45b81c045849d8fb16c9193571e-5"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">.</span></span><span data-offset-key="64d6b45b81c045849d8fb16c9193571e-6"><span class="prism-token token  function ">getState</span></span><span data-offset-key="64d6b45b81c045849d8fb16c9193571e-7"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">())</span></span></span></div><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="f8ca55ceee554994ba9ce9b08a381425"><span data-key="1ed1370f48b648f6938bb6297925666d"><span data-offset-key="1ed1370f48b648f6938bb6297925666d-0"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">)</span></span></span></div><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="78b9ee8742fd4499bce65b9da1d6d8d1"><span data-key="94ce7b2efaf24c3fa7ee5432ce786610"><span data-offset-key="94ce7b2efaf24c3fa7ee5432ce786610-0"><span data-slate-zero-width="true"> </span></span></span></div><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="b48cfbe225584c99a4419646d9ca78b3"><span data-key="ffbfd45102804bc89da9a09594ffe69f"><span data-offset-key="ffbfd45102804bc89da9a09594ffe69f-0"><span class="prism-token token  comment ">// The only way to mutate the internal state is to dispatch an action.</span></span></span></div><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="80fb6f14d2224f1e86d0a2d5c1d606c5"><span data-key="2baafa3fe77147feb656612db9f9cd12"><span data-offset-key="2baafa3fe77147feb656612db9f9cd12-0"><span class="prism-token token  comment ">// The actions can be serialized, logged or stored and later replayed.</span></span></span></div><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="9b8253a225574c7cba54c4983ce65ae5"><span data-key="9e2a1838e3c049cf95bbc5d41b3092ae"><span data-offset-key="9e2a1838e3c049cf95bbc5d41b3092ae-0">store</span><span data-offset-key="9e2a1838e3c049cf95bbc5d41b3092ae-1"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">.</span></span><span data-offset-key="9e2a1838e3c049cf95bbc5d41b3092ae-2"><span class="prism-token token  function ">dispatch</span></span><span data-offset-key="9e2a1838e3c049cf95bbc5d41b3092ae-3"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">({</span></span><span data-offset-key="9e2a1838e3c049cf95bbc5d41b3092ae-4"> type</span><span data-offset-key="9e2a1838e3c049cf95bbc5d41b3092ae-5"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">:</span></span><span data-offset-key="9e2a1838e3c049cf95bbc5d41b3092ae-6"> </span><span data-offset-key="9e2a1838e3c049cf95bbc5d41b3092ae-7"><span class="prism-token token  string ">&#x27;INCREMENT&#x27;</span></span><span data-offset-key="9e2a1838e3c049cf95bbc5d41b3092ae-8"> </span><span data-offset-key="9e2a1838e3c049cf95bbc5d41b3092ae-9"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">})</span></span></span></div><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="6bb6e6ac6d7e46c59eebbfaef6108fb8"><span data-key="79e42f91263d4a7b9367097081f59a4b"><span data-offset-key="79e42f91263d4a7b9367097081f59a4b-0"><span class="prism-token token  comment ">// 1</span></span></span></div><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="7026e9859eed42729e4da7e3a3df8115"><span data-key="bba8d789527e416aa9c709786177c206"><span data-offset-key="bba8d789527e416aa9c709786177c206-0">store</span><span data-offset-key="bba8d789527e416aa9c709786177c206-1"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">.</span></span><span data-offset-key="bba8d789527e416aa9c709786177c206-2"><span class="prism-token token  function ">dispatch</span></span><span data-offset-key="bba8d789527e416aa9c709786177c206-3"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">({</span></span><span data-offset-key="bba8d789527e416aa9c709786177c206-4"> type</span><span data-offset-key="bba8d789527e416aa9c709786177c206-5"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">:</span></span><span data-offset-key="bba8d789527e416aa9c709786177c206-6"> </span><span data-offset-key="bba8d789527e416aa9c709786177c206-7"><span class="prism-token token  string ">&#x27;INCREMENT&#x27;</span></span><span data-offset-key="bba8d789527e416aa9c709786177c206-8"> </span><span data-offset-key="bba8d789527e416aa9c709786177c206-9"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">})</span></span></span></div><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="1df8c4f4b26845a29ffb6dea2b95e92f"><span data-key="70701b7231be4d338809e50301d82471"><span data-offset-key="70701b7231be4d338809e50301d82471-0"><span class="prism-token token  comment ">// 2</span></span></span></div><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="72696a3045364d32849db7e04eccee86"><span data-key="4560ea9b2b574a9692db585e2fe76645"><span data-offset-key="4560ea9b2b574a9692db585e2fe76645-0">store</span><span data-offset-key="4560ea9b2b574a9692db585e2fe76645-1"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">.</span></span><span data-offset-key="4560ea9b2b574a9692db585e2fe76645-2"><span class="prism-token token  function ">dispatch</span></span><span data-offset-key="4560ea9b2b574a9692db585e2fe76645-3"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">({</span></span><span data-offset-key="4560ea9b2b574a9692db585e2fe76645-4"> type</span><span data-offset-key="4560ea9b2b574a9692db585e2fe76645-5"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">:</span></span><span data-offset-key="4560ea9b2b574a9692db585e2fe76645-6"> </span><span data-offset-key="4560ea9b2b574a9692db585e2fe76645-7"><span class="prism-token token  string ">&#x27;DECREMENT&#x27;</span></span><span data-offset-key="4560ea9b2b574a9692db585e2fe76645-8"> </span><span data-offset-key="4560ea9b2b574a9692db585e2fe76645-9"><span class="prism-token token  punctuation ">})</span></span></span></div><div class="_17r7t1h" data-key="acfa5075fadd4f09b707777c5814ffea"><span data-key="854490a7b6d9465f8f157cb974382a75"><span data-offset-key="854490a7b6d9465f8f157cb974382a75-0"><span class="prism-token token  comment ">// 1</span></span></span></div></pre></div></div></div><p class="_v011fo" data-key="d0732aed2bf74c9e9b584ca3d4e0096c"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="f99fa2c10a0747188d4bb5c73c6ff97b"><span data-offset-key="f99fa2c10a0747188d4bb5c73c6ff97b-0">Instead of mutating the state directly, you specify the mutations you want to happen with plain objects called </span><span data-offset-key="f99fa2c10a0747188d4bb5c73c6ff97b-1"><em>actions</em></span><span data-offset-key="f99fa2c10a0747188d4bb5c73c6ff97b-2">. Then you write a special function called a </span><span data-offset-key="f99fa2c10a0747188d4bb5c73c6ff97b-3"><em>reducer</em></span><span data-offset-key="f99fa2c10a0747188d4bb5c73c6ff97b-4"> to decide how every action transforms the entire application&#x27;s state.</span></span></span></p><p class="_v011fo" data-key="d7524d28c0184637b7bb1faf53623da3"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="37e04ec05da244bdae9224aaac4cebe4"><span data-offset-key="37e04ec05da244bdae9224aaac4cebe4-0">If you&#x27;re coming from Flux, there is a single important difference you need to understand. Redux doesn&#x27;t have a Dispatcher or support many stores. Instead, there is just a single store with a single root reducing function. As your app grows, instead of adding stores, you split the root reducer into smaller reducers independently operating on the different parts of the state tree. This is exactly like how there is just one root component in a React app, but it is composed out of many small components.</span></span></span></p><p class="_v011fo" data-key="739df944db4649fc851aa597c46090a0"><span class="_1yjweog"><span data-key="2ec93c689f9d43efb1322aa0140bd94c"><span data-offset-key="2ec93c689f9d43efb1322aa0140bd94c-0">This architecture might seem like an overkill for a counter app, but the beauty of this pattern is how well it scales to large and complex apps. It also enables very powerful developer tools, because it is possible to trace every mutation to the action that caused it. You can record user sessions and reproduce them just by replaying every action.</span></span></span></p><h1 id="learn-redux-from-its-creator" class="_8yc956y" data-key="985a9dc236954e46b5a2951b07fd4b37"><div class="_bc4egv"><span class="_1a3b01i"><span data-key="7a305993bd3d44778030daf063cc8ea0"><span done.</span></span></span></p><h1 id="documentation" class="_8yc956y" data-key="fa1e0aa56a384f698d70e7c4043e48dc"><div class="_bc4egv"><span class="_1a3b01i"><span data-key="5e1d748dee9d43209d54983694a69918"><span data-offset-key="5e1d748dee9d43209d54983694a69918-0">Documentation</span></span></span><a href="#documentation" contenteditable="false" class="_i422ldx"><span class="_15qrizw"><svg preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet" height="1em" width="1em" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" stroke="none" Redux doesn't have a Dispatcher or support many stores. Instead, there is just a single store with a single root reducing function. As your app grows, instead of adding stores, you split the root reducer into smaller reducers independently operating on the different parts of the state tree. This is exactly like how there is just one root component in a React app, but it is composed out of many small components."}]}]},{"kind":"block","type":"paragraph","key":"739df944db4649fc851aa597c46090a0","isVoid":false,"data":{},"nodes":[{"kind":"text","key":"2ec93c689f9d43efb1322aa0140bd94c","ranges":[{"kind":"range","marks":[],"text":"This architecture might seem like an overkill for a counter app, but the beauty of this pattern is how well it scales to large and complex apps.
